[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Stress at work:

**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand the stress levels and experiences of employees at work. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve to create a healthier and more productive work environment.

**Section 1: Demographics**

1. What is your job title?
2. How many years have you been working at our company?
3. What is your age range?
4. What is your department/ team?

**Section 2: Stress Levels**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your overall stress level at work? (1 = Very Low, 5 = Very High)
2. How often do you feel stressed at work? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)
3. Which of the following best describes your stress level during peak work hours? (Select all that apply)
	* I feel calm and focused
	* I feel moderately stressed
	* I feel highly stressed
	* I feel overwhelmed
4. Have you experienced any physical symptoms of stress at work (e.g., headaches, fatigue, muscle tension)? (Yes/No)

**Section 3: Stressors**

1. Which of the following work-related factors contributes most to your stress levels? (Rank in order of importance)
	* Workload
	* Deadlines
	* Lack of control
	* Conflicting priorities
	* Communication issues
	* Other (please specify)
2. Have you experienced any of the following stressors at work? (Yes/No)
	* Unrealistic expectations
	* Lack of recognition
	* Poor work-life balance
	* Conflicting values
	* Other (please specify)
3. How often do you feel undervalued or unappreciated at work? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

**Section 4: Coping Mechanisms**

1. How do you typically cope with stress at work? (Select all that apply)
	* Take a break
	* Exercise
	* Talk to a colleague or supervisor
	* Practice mindfulness
	* Seek professional help
	* Other (please specify)
2. Have you noticed any changes in your coping mechanisms over time? (Yes/No)
3. How effective do you think your coping mechanisms are in managing stress at work? (Scale: 1 = Not Very Effective, 2 = Somewhat Effective, 3 = Very Effective, 4 = Extremely Effective)

**Section 5: Suggestions**

1. What do you think would help reduce stress at work? (Open-ended question)
2. Are there any changes or initiatives you would like to see implemented to improve work-life balance? (Open-ended question)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire. Your responses will help us better understand the stress levels and experiences of employees at work. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

I hope this helps! Let me know if you'd like me to convert it into a specific format.

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your opinion and want to understand your experiences and perceptions about our workplace environment. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more comfortable and productive work environment for everyone.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the overall workplace environment?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What do you like most about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What do you like least about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Physical Workspace**

4. How would you rate the cleanliness and organization of your workspace?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Fair, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

5. Are there any physical aspects of your workspace that cause discomfort or distraction? (e.g., lighting, temperature, noise)

(Open-ended text field)

6. Do you have a dedicated workspace or shared workspace? If shared, how do you feel about it?

(1 = Very Positive, 2 = Somewhat Positive, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Negative, 5 = Very Negative)

**Section 3: Social Environment**

7. How would you rate the level of collaboration and teamwork among colleagues?

(1 = Very Low, 2 = Low, 3 = Medium, 4 = High, 5 = Very High)

8. Are there any social or cultural aspects of the workplace that you find uncomfortable or distracting? (e.g., noise levels, office politics)

(Open-ended text field)

9. Do you feel like you have a sense of community or belonging in the workplace?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 4: Technology and Tools**

10. How would you rate the effectiveness of our technology and tools in supporting your work?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Fair, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

11. Are there any technology or tool-related issues that cause frustration or inefficiency?

(Open-ended text field)

12. Do you have the necessary resources and support to perform your job effectively?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

13. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a better workplace environment for everyone.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Remote working experience:

**Remote Working Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As we continue to explore the benefits and challenges of remote working, we want to hear from you about your experiences. Your input will help us better understand the impact of remote work on our team's productivity, communication, and overall job satisfaction.

**Section 1: General Information**

1. What is your current role at the company?
2. How long have you been working remotely (in months)?
3. What is your typical work schedule (e.g., 9-to-5, flexible hours, etc.)?

**Section 2: Remote Work Experience**

4. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your overall experience with remote working?

(1 = Very Negative, 2 = Somewhat Negative, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Positive, 5 = Very Positive)

5. What are the top three benefits you've experienced while working remotely?

6. What are the top three challenges you've faced while working remotely?

7. How often do you feel disconnected from the team or lack of face-to-face interaction?

(Scale: 1 = Almost Always, 2 = Often, 3 = Sometimes, 4 = Rarely, 5 = Almost Never)

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

8. How do you currently communicate with your team and manager while working remotely?

(Select all that apply: Email, Video Conferencing, Instant Messaging, Phone Calls, In-Person Meetings)

9. Have you experienced any difficulties with communication or collaboration while working remotely?

(Yes/No)

10. If yes, please describe the challenges you've faced and how you've overcome them.

**Section 4: Productivity and Work-Life Balance**

11. How has your productivity changed since starting remote work?

(Select one: Increased, Decreased, Remained the Same)

12. Do you find it easier or harder to separate work and personal life while working remotely?

(Select one: Easier, Harder, No Difference)

13. How often do you work outside of regular working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends)?

(Scale: 1 = Almost Always, 2 = Often, 3 = Sometimes, 4 = Rarely, 5 = Almost Never)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

14. Is there anything you'd like to share about your remote working experience that wasn't covered in this questionnaire?

15. Do you have any suggestions for improving the remote working experience within our company?

**Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences! Your input is invaluable in helping us shape our remote working policies and practices.**

Here is a sample questionnaire on End of working relationship:

**End of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather feedback and insights on the end of working relationships at our company. Your responses will help us understand the reasons, experiences, and outcomes of these transitions. Your anonymity is guaranteed.

**Section 1: Background Information**

1. What is your current role at the company? (Select one)
	* Employee
	* Manager
	* HR Representative
	* Other (please specify)
2. How long have you been with the company?
	* Less than 6 months
	* 6 months to 1 year
	* 1-2 years
	* 2-5 years
	* More than 5 years

**Section 2: End of Working Relationship Experience**

1. Have you been involved in an end of working relationship (e.g., termination, resignation, layoff) in the past 12 months?
	* Yes
	* No
2. If yes, what was the reason for the end of working relationship? (Select all that apply)
	* Performance issues
	* Job elimination or restructuring
	* Company downsizing
	* Voluntary resignation
	* Other (please specify)
3. How would you rate the overall experience of the end of working relationship?
	* Very positive
	* Somewhat positive
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat negative
	* Very negative

**Section 3: Communication and Support**

1. How would you rate the communication from HR and management during the end of working relationship process?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
	* Very poor
2. Did you receive adequate support during the transition period?
	* Yes
	* No
3. What kind of support would you have liked to receive during the transition period? (Select all that apply)
	* Career counseling
	* Job placement assistance
	* Outplacement services
	* Emotional support
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Outcomes and Suggestions**

1. How would you rate the overall outcome of the end of working relationship?
	* Very positive
	* Somewhat positive
	* Neutral
	* Somewhat negative
	* Very negative
2. Do you have any suggestions for improving the end of working relationship process at our company?
	* (Open-ended text field)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback on the end of working relationship process at our company. Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our processes and support our employees.

Please let me know if you would like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format (e.g., Google Forms, Microsoft Word, etc.).

**Access to Technology and Tools Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve our work environment and employee satisfaction, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on access to technology and tools within the company. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and make informed decisions to support your work.

**Section 1: Current Technology and Tool Usage**

1. How often do you use technology and tools for work purposes?

a) Daily
b) Several times a week
c) Occasionally
d) Rarely

2. Which of the following technologies and tools do you use most frequently? (Select all that apply)

a) Computer/Laptop
b) Mobile Device
c) Software Applications (e.g., Microsoft Office, Google Workspace)
d) Collaboration Tools (e.g., Slack, Trello)
e) Other (please specify)

3. Are there any technology or tools that you find difficult to access or use?

a) Yes
b) No

**Section 2: Barriers to Access**

4. What are the main barriers you face when trying to access technology and tools? (Select all that apply)

a) Lack of training or support
b) Technical issues or glitches
c) Limited availability or accessibility
d) Prioritization of other tasks or responsibilities
e) Other (please specify)

5. Have you ever experienced any of the following issues when trying to access technology and tools? (Select all that apply)

a) Slow or unreliable internet connection
b) Outdated or incompatible software
c) Limited printing or scanning capabilities
d) Difficulty logging in or accessing accounts
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Suggestions and Ideas**

6. What would you like to see improved or added in terms of technology and tools to support your work?

7. Are there any specific technologies or tools that you think would greatly benefit your work or role? (Select all that apply)

a) Project management tools
b) Communication and collaboration tools
c) Data analysis and visualization tools
d) Creative design and editing tools
e) Other (please specify)

8. Do you have any suggestions for how we can better support your technology and tool needs?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and opinions on access to technology and tools. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more effective and efficient work environment. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

I hope this helps! Let me know if you'd like me to convert it to a specific format or make any changes.

**Access to Technology and Tools Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**

b) Mobile Devices (Smartphones/Tablets)
c) Software Applications (e.g., Microsoft Office, Google Suite)

Here's a questionnaire on Benefits:

**Benefits Perception Survey**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve employee satisfaction and engagement, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on the benefits we offer. Your input will help us understand what matters most to you and make informed decisions about our benefits program.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the benefits package offered by our company?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What do you like most about our benefits package?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What do you like least about our benefits package?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Health and Wellness**

1. How important is it to you that our company offers a comprehensive health insurance plan?

(Scale: 1 = Not Important at All, 2 = Somewhat Important, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Important, 5 = Very Important)

2. Have you used any of our wellness programs or services (e.g., gym membership, mental health resources)? If so, what did you think of them?

(Open-ended text field)

3. Would you like to see more wellness programs or services offered by our company?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 3: Financial Benefits**

1. How important is it to you that our company offers a 401(k) or other retirement savings plan?

(Scale: 1 = Not Important at All, 2 = Somewhat Important, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Important, 5 = Very Important)

2. Have you participated in our company's stock purchase plan or other financial benefits program? If so, what did you think of it?

(Open-ended text field)

3. Would you like to see more financial benefits or incentives offered by our company?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 4: Other Benefits**

1. How important is it to you that our company offers flexible work arrangements (e.g., telecommuting, flexible hours)?

(Scale: 1 = Not Important at All, 2 = Somewhat Important, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Important, 5 = Very Important)

2. Have you used any of our company's family-friendly benefits (e.g., parental leave, adoption assistance)? If so, what did you think of them?

(Open-ended text field)

3. Would you like to see more family-friendly benefits or services offered by our company?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

Is there anything else you'd like to share about our benefits package or any suggestions you have for improving it?

(Open-ended text field)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a benefits program that supports your needs and well-being.

**Employee Motivation Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**

**Section 1: Job Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job?

(1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. What are the most important factors that contribute to your job satisfaction? (Select all that apply)

* Sense of accomplishment
* Opportunities for growth and development
* Good work-life balance
* Positive work environment
* Recognition and rewards
* Other (please specify)

3. Have you experienced a significant increase or decrease in job satisfaction over the past 6 months? If so, what contributed to the change?

**Section 2: Motivators and Demotivators**

4. What motivates you to come to work every day? (Select all that apply)

* Sense of purpose and meaning
* Desire to learn and grow
* Recognition and appreciation
* Opportunities for advancement
* Autonomy and independence
* Other (please specify)

5. What demotivates you at work? (Select all that apply)

* Lack of challenge or opportunities for growth
* Poor communication or unclear expectations
* Unsupportive or unsympathetic management
* Unfair treatment or favoritism
* Unhappiness with work-life balance
* Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Recognition and Rewards**

6. How often do you feel recognized and appreciated for your work?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost always, 5 = Always)

7. What types of recognition or rewards would you find most motivating? (Select all that apply)

* Public recognition or praise
* Monetary rewards or bonuses
* Additional time off or flexible scheduling
* Professional development opportunities
* Title or role changes
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Feedback and Communication**

8. How often do you receive constructive feedback on your performance?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost always, 5 = Always)

9. How would you like to receive feedback on your performance? (Select all that apply)

* Regular check-ins with manager
* Written performance reviews
* Peer feedback or coaching
* Self-assessment and reflection
* Other (please specify)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

10. Is there anything else you'd like to share about what motivates or demotivates you at work?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide additional comments or suggestions)

Here's a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms:

**Feedback Mechanisms Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your opinion and want to understand how you currently receive and provide feedback within the organization. Your responses will help us improve our feedback mechanisms and create a more open and collaborative work environment.

**Section 1: Current Feedback Practices**

1. How often do you receive feedback from your supervisor or manager?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Quarterly
e) Rarely

2. What types of feedback do you typically receive? (Select all that apply)

a) Performance feedback
b) Constructive criticism
c) Recognition and praise
d) Suggestions for improvement
e) Other (please specify)

3. How do you currently provide feedback to your supervisor or manager?

a) Regularly scheduled meetings
b) Informal check-ins
c) Written reports or emails
d) Verbal conversations
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Desired Feedback Mechanisms**

1. What feedback mechanisms would you like to see implemented within the organization? (Select all that apply)

a) Regular 1-on-1 meetings with supervisors
b) Anonymous feedback system
c) Online feedback platform
d) Regular team meetings for feedback and discussion
e) Other (please specify)

2. How important is it for you to receive feedback in a timely manner?

a) Very important
b) Somewhat important
c) Not very important
d) Not at all important

3. Would you prefer to receive feedback in a specific format (e.g., written, verbal, visual)? If so, please specify.

**Section 3: Barriers to Effective Feedback**

1. What barriers do you face when trying to provide or receive feedback within the organization? (Select all that apply)

a) Fear of negative consequences
b) Lack of time or resources
c) Unclear expectations or goals
d) Difficulty articulating feedback
e) Other (please specify)

2. How do you think the organization could overcome these barriers?

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

Is there anything else you'd like to share about feedback mechanisms within the organization?

3. Would you prefer to receive feedback in a specific format (e.g., written, verbal, visual)? If so, please specify.

**Section 3: Barriers to Feedback**

1. What barriers do you face when providing or receiving feedback? (Select all that apply)

a) Fear of negative consequences
b) Lack of time
c) Unclear expectations
d) Difficulty articulating feedback
e) Other (please specify)

2. How do you think the organization could overcome these barriers?

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

Is there anything else you'd like to share about feedback mechanisms within the organization?

**Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our feedback mechanisms.**

b) No

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide specific suggestions)

2. Are there any specific health and safety concerns or issues that you would like to see addressed?

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide specific suggestions)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities:

**Internal Mobility Opportunities Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to support employee growth and development, we're interested in understanding your experiences and perceptions regarding internal mobility opportunities within the company. Your input will help us identify areas for improvement and create more effective programs to support your career advancement.

**Section 1: Current Job Satisfaction and Mobility Aspirations**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job role?

(1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. How important is internal mobility to you? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not important at all" and 5 is "very important")

3. What motivates you to consider internal mobility opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Career advancement
* New challenges and responsibilities
* Desire to learn new skills
* Desire to work in a different department or team
* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Barriers to Internal Mobility**

1. What do you think is the biggest barrier to internal mobility within the company? (Select all that apply)

* Lack of awareness about available opportunities
* Limited job openings or competition for roles
* Fear of change or uncertainty
* Lack of support or resources for career development
* Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever considered applying for an internal job opening, but decided not to? If so, what was the reason?

3. Do you feel that the company provides adequate support and resources for employees to develop their skills and advance their careers? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "strongly disagree" and 5 is "strongly agree")

**Section 3: Preferred Internal Mobility Channels**

1. Which of the following internal mobility channels would you prefer to use to explore new opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Company-wide job postings
* Departmental job postings
* Employee referrals
* Mentorship programs
* Career development workshops
* Other (please specify)

2. Would you prefer to receive internal job postings and career development opportunities through:

* Email notifications
* Company intranet
* Social media platforms
* Mobile app
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

1. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about internal mobility opportunities within the company?

2. Are there any specific skills or training programs you would like to see offered to support internal mobility?

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences with us! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and developmental environment for our employees.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness:

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve leadership development and effectiveness, we would like to gather your feedback on the leadership styles and behaviors that are most effective in our organization. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and weakness, and inform our training and development programs.

**Section 1: Leadership Style**

1. When faced with a difficult decision, what do you typically rely on to make a choice?

a) Logic and analysis
b) Intuition and gut feeling
c) Input from others
d) A combination of the above

2. How would you describe your leadership style?

a) Autocratic (making decisions without input from others)
b) Democratic (involving others in decision-making)
c) Laissez-faire (giving others a lot of autonomy)
d) Transformational (inspiring and motivating others)

3. What motivates you to take action as a leader?

a) Achieving specific goals and objectives
b) Building strong relationships with team members
c) Creating a positive work culture
d) All of the above

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate your communication style?

a) Clear and concise
b) Open and transparent
c) Direct and assertive
d) Indirect and subtle

5. What do you think is the most effective way to communicate with your team?

a) Regular meetings and updates
b) One-on-one check-ins and feedback
c) Written reports and emails
d) A combination of the above

6. How do you handle conflict or disagreements within your team?

a) Addressing the issue directly and openly
b) Mediating and facilitating a resolution
c) Avoiding the issue and hoping it resolves itself
d) Escalating the issue to a higher authority

**Section 3: Decision-Making**

7. What factors do you consider when making decisions as a leader?

a) Data and analytics
b) Expert opinions and advice
c) Stakeholder input and feedback
d) A combination of the above

8. How do you prioritize tasks and allocate resources?

a) Based on urgency and importance
b) Based on strategic alignment and impact
c) Based on team member input and feedback
d) Based on personal judgment and intuition

9. What do you do when faced with a decision that has no clear right or wrong answer?

a) Seek input from others
b) Trust your instincts and make a decision
c) Delay the decision and gather more information
d) Avoid making a decision and punt the issue

**Section 4: Team Development**

a) Clear goals and objectives
b) Strong relationships and trust
c) Effective communication and feedback
d) A combination of the above

11. How do you approach developing and coaching your team members?

a) Providing regular feedback and guidance
b) Offering training and development opportunities
c) Encouraging self-directed learning and growth
d) A combination of the above

12. What do you think is the most effective way to recognize and reward team members?

a) Public recognition and praise
b) Monetary rewards and incentives
c) Additional responsibilities and challenges
d) A combination of the above

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve leadership development and effectiveness, we would like to gather your feedback on the leadership styles and behaviors that are most effective in our organization. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and weakness, and inform our training and development programs.

**Section 1: Leadership Style**

1. When faced with a difficult decision, what do you typically rely on to make a choice?

a) Logic and analysis
b) Intuition and gut feeling
c) Input from others
d) A combination of the above

2. How would you describe your leadership style?

a) Autocratic (making decisions without input from others)
b) Democratic (involving others in decision-making)
c) Laissez-faire (giving others a lot of autonomy)
d) Transformational (inspiring and motivating others)

3. What motivates you to take action as a leader?

a) Achieving specific goals and objectives
b) Building strong relationships with team members
c) Creating a positive work culture
d) All of the above

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate your communication style?

a) Clear and concise
b) Open and transparent
c) Direct and assertive
d) Indirect and subtle

5. What do you think is the most effective way to communicate with your team?

a) Regular meetings and updates
b) One-on-one check-ins and feedback
c) Written reports and emails
d) A combination of the above

6. How do you handle conflict or disagreements within your team?

a) Addressing the issue directly and openly
b) Mediating and facilitating a resolution
c) Avoiding the issue and hoping it resolves itself
d) Escalating the issue to a higher authority

**Section 3: Decision-Making**

7. What factors do you consider when making decisions as a leader?

a) Data and analytics
b) Expert opinions and advice
c) Stakeholder input and feedback
d) A combination of the above

8. How do you prioritize tasks and allocate resources?

a) Based on urgency and importance
b) Based on strategic alignment and impact
c) Based on team member input and feedback
d) Based on personal judgment and intuition

9. What do you do when faced with a decision that has no clear right or wrong answer?

a) Seek input from others
b) Trust your instincts and make a decision
c) Delay the decision and gather more information
d) Avoid making a decision and punt the issue

**Section 4: Team Development**

10. What do you think is the most important factor in building a high-performing team?

c) Effective communication and feedback

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding Experience**

1. How did you first learn about our company and the job opportunity that led you to apply?
	* I saw a job posting online
	* I was referred by a friend or colleague
	* I saw an advertisement on social media
	* I saw a job posting on a job board
	* Other (please specify)
2. What were your expectations about the onboarding process before starting your new role?
	* I expected a formal orientation program
	* I expected to meet with my supervisor and HR representative
	* I expected to receive a comprehensive employee handbook
	* I expected to start working on my first tasks immediately
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

1. How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our onboarding process?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
	* Very Poor
2. What did you find most helpful during the onboarding process?
	* Meeting with my supervisor and HR representative
	* Receiving a comprehensive employee handbook
	* Completing online training modules
	* Meeting with colleagues and getting familiar with the team
	* Other (please specify)
3. What did you find most challenging during the onboarding process?

	* Meeting new people and building relationships
	* Feeling overwhelmed with too much information

**Pressure at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding the pressures you face at work and how they impact your job satisfaction and overall well-being. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can provide support and make improvements.

**Section 1: Perceived Pressure**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost always, 5 = Always)

2. Which of the following best describes your experience with pressure at work?

a) I often feel like I'm drowning in tasks and responsibilities.
b) I sometimes feel like I'm struggling to keep up, but I manage.
c) I rarely feel pressured, and I'm able to handle my workload easily.
d) Other (please specify)

3. How do you typically respond to pressure at work?

a) I try to tackle the task head-on and push through.
b) I take a step back, prioritize, and focus on the most important tasks.
c) I get anxious and stressed, but I try to manage my emotions.
d) I feel overwhelmed and unsure of how to proceed.

**Section 2: Impact on Job Satisfaction**

4. How does pressure at work affect your job satisfaction?

a) It has a significant negative impact.
b) It has a moderate negative impact.
c) It has a minor negative impact.
d) It has no impact.

5. Have you ever considered leaving your job due to pressure at work?

a) Yes, I've thought about it.
b) No, I haven't thought about it.
c) Maybe, it depends on the situation.

**Section 3: Coping Mechanisms**

6. What coping mechanisms do you use to manage pressure at work?

a) I take regular breaks and prioritize self-care.
b) I delegate tasks and ask for help when needed.
c) I focus on the task at hand and try to stay focused.
d) I try to avoid thinking about it and hope it goes away.

7. How often do you take time off or use vacation days to recharge?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost always, 5 = Always)

**Section 4: Suggestions for Improvement**

8. What changes would you suggest to reduce pressure at work?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide suggestions)

9. Are there any specific resources or support systems you think would help you manage pressure at work?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide suggestions)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your experiences with pressure at work. Your input will help us better understand the pressures you face and identify areas where we can provide support and make improvements.

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely
e) Never

2. What types of recognition do you value most? (Select all that apply)

a) Public recognition (e.g., company-wide announcements)
b) Private recognition (e.g., one-on-one feedback)
c) Monetary rewards (e.g., bonuses, gift cards)
d) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible work arrangements)
e) Other (please specify)

3. Have you received a recognition or reward in the past 6 months? If yes, please describe.

**Section 2: Desired Recognition and Rewards**

1. What would make you feel most recognized and valued in your role?

(Open-ended text field)

2. Are there any specific recognition or reward programs you'd like to see implemented? If yes, please describe.

(Open-ended text field)

3. Would you prefer recognition and rewards to be:

a) Individualized (e.g., tailored to your specific achievements)
b) Team-based (e.g., recognizing team efforts)
c) Both individualized and team-based
d) Neither individualized nor team-based

**Section 3: Barriers to Recognition and Rewards**

1. What barriers do you face in feeling recognized and rewarded? (Select all that apply)

a) Lack of transparency in recognition and reward processes
b) Limited opportunities for recognition and rewards
c) Perceived favoritism or bias in recognition and reward decisions
d) Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever felt undervalued or unappreciated despite your efforts? If yes, please describe.

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving our recognition and rewards programs?

(Open-ended text field)

(Open-ended text field)

**Roadmap Planning Feedback Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your input in helping us improve our roadmap planning process. Your feedback will help us refine our approach to better align with the company's goals and priorities. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. How would you rate your overall satisfaction with the roadmap planning process?

a) Very Satisfied
b) Somewhat Satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat Dissatisfied
e) Very Dissatisfied

2. What did you like most about the roadmap planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What did you like least about the roadmap planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate the communication from the planning team during the roadmap planning process?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor
e) Very Poor

5. Were you kept informed about changes to the roadmap or priorities?

a) Yes, I was well-informed
b) Mostly, but there were some surprises
c) Not very well-informed
d) Not at all informed

6. Were there any unclear or confusing aspects of the roadmap or planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 3: Prioritization**

7. How would you rate the prioritization of features or initiatives in the roadmap?

a) Well-prioritized
b) Mostly well-prioritized
c) Priorities were unclear or confusing
d) Priorities were not well-considered

8. Were there any features or initiatives that you felt were not well-prioritized or overlooked?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 4: Collaboration**

9. How would you rate the collaboration and coordination with other teams or stakeholders during the roadmap planning process?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor
e) Very Poor

10. Were there any challenges or obstacles that hindered collaboration or coordination during the roadmap planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 5: Additional Feedback**

11. Do you have any additional feedback or suggestions for improving the roadmap planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

12. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your experience with the roadmap planning process?

(Open-ended text field)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our roadmap planning process.

**Satisfaction Survey**

**Introduction:**
We value your opinion and want to understand your level of satisfaction with your experience at [Company Name]. Your feedback will help us identify areas of strength and opportunities for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your overall experience at [Company Name]?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What are the most important factors that contribute to your overall satisfaction at [Company Name]? (Select all that apply)

* Job responsibilities and challenges
* Work-life balance
* Communication with management and colleagues
* Opportunities for growth and development
* Company culture and values
* Compensation and benefits
* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Job Responsibilities and Challenges**

1. How would you rate the level of challenge and engagement in your current role?

(1 = Very Low, 2 = Low, 3 = Medium, 4 = High, 5 = Very High)

2. Are there any specific aspects of your job that you find particularly satisfying or dissatisfying? (Open-ended question)

**Section 3: Communication and Feedback**

1. How would you rate the quality of communication from management and colleagues?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Fair, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

2. Do you feel that you receive regular and constructive feedback on your performance?

(Yes/No)

**Section 4: Company Culture and Values**

1. How would you rate the alignment of [Company Name]'s values and mission with your own personal values and goals?

(1 = Not at All, 2 = Somewhat, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat, 5 = Very)

2. Are there any specific aspects of [Company Name]'s culture that you find particularly appealing or unappealing? (Open-ended question)

**Section 5: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

1. Is there anything that you would like to see changed or improved at [Company Name]?

(Open-ended question)

2. Do you have any suggestions for how [Company Name] can better support your growth and development?

(Open-ended question)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve and grow as a company.

**Section 3: Training and Development Challenges**

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather feedback on our company's training and development programs. Your input will help us understand the effectiveness of our programs and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: Current Training and Development Programs**

1. Which of the following training and development programs have you participated in within the past 12 months? (Select all that apply)

	* Leadership development
	* Technical skills training
	* Soft skills training (e.g., communication, teamwork)
	* Industry-specific training
	* Other (please specify)

2. How would you rate the overall quality of the training and development programs you've participated in?

	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
	* Not applicable

3. What do you think is the most valuable aspect of our training and development programs? (Select one)

	* Practical application of skills
	* Networking opportunities
	* Access to industry experts
	* Opportunities for career advancement
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Training and Development Needs**

1. What skills or knowledge do you think would be most beneficial for you to acquire or improve in the next 12 months? (Select all that apply)

	* Leadership and management
	* Technical skills (e.g., software, tools)
	* Communication and interpersonal skills
	* Time management and organization
	* Industry-specific knowledge
	* Other (please specify)

2. Are there any specific training or development programs you would like to see offered in the next 12 months? If so, please describe.

3. How important is it for you to have opportunities for training and development within the company? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not important at all" and 5 is "very important")

**Section 3: Training and Development Challenges**

1. What challenges do you face in terms of accessing or utilizing training and development opportunities within the company? (Select all that apply)

	* Limited availability of training programs
	* Scheduling conflicts
	* Lack of awareness about training opportunities
	* Limited access to training resources (e.g., budget constraints)
	* Other (please specify)

2. How do you think we could improve the training and development programs to better meet your needs?

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about our training and development programs?

2. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your training and development experiences within the company?

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our training and development programs.

Here's a sample questionnaire on WorkLife Balance:

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your responses will help us understand the current state of worklife balance within our organization and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses if you'd like.

**Section 1: Perceptions of WorkLife Balance**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your current worklife balance?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

2. Do you feel that your work demands are impacting your personal life?

a) Yes, often
b) Yes, sometimes
c) No, not at all

3. How often do you find yourself working outside of regular working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends)?

a) Frequently
b) Occasionally
c) Rarely
d) Never

**Section 2: Time Management and Prioritization**

4. How do you prioritize your tasks and responsibilities?

a) I prioritize tasks based on urgency and importance
b) I prioritize tasks based on personal goals and values
c) I prioritize tasks based on company expectations and deadlines
d) Other (please specify)

5. How many hours do you typically work per week?

(Open-ended response)

6. Do you feel that you have enough time for personal activities and hobbies?

a) Yes, I have plenty of time
b) Yes, I have some time
c) No, I don't have enough time

**Section 3: Support Systems and Resources**

7. Do you feel supported by your manager and colleagues in achieving a healthy worklife balance?

a) Yes, I feel very supported
b) Yes, I feel somewhat supported
c) No, I don't feel supported

8. Are there any company resources or programs that you feel would help you achieve a better worklife balance?

(Open-ended response)

9. Would you like to see more flexible work arrangements (e.g., telecommuting, flexible hours) offered by the company?

a) Yes, I would like to see more options
b) No, I'm happy with the current options
c) Undecided

**Section 4: Suggestions and Feedback**

10. What do you think the company could do to improve worklife balance for employees?

(Open-ended response)

11. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about worklife balance in our organization?

(Open-ended response)

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a better worklife balance for all employees.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Workload Management:

**Workload Management Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand your experiences and perceptions about workload management within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to enhance workload management.

**Section 1: Current Workload**

1. On average, how many tasks or projects do you typically handle at any given time?

a) 1-3
b) 4-6
c) 7-10
d) More than 10

2. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

a) Rarely
b) Occasionally
c) Frequently
d) Almost always

3. What is the most common type of task or project you handle? (Select all that apply)

a) Routine administrative tasks
b) Special projects or initiatives
c) Customer-facing tasks
d) Team or departmental responsibilities
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Time Management**

4. How do you prioritize your tasks and projects?

a) Based on urgency and importance
b) Based on deadlines and timelines
c) Based on personal preference and interest
d) Based on input from others (e.g., manager, team members)

5. What tools or methods do you use to manage your time effectively? (Select all that apply)

a) To-do lists
b) Calendars
c) Task management software
d) Pomodoro timers
e) Other (please specify)

6. How often do you take breaks or practice self-care to manage stress and workload?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

7. How often do you communicate with your team or manager about your workload and priorities?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely

8. What challenges do you face when collaborating with others on projects or tasks? (Select all that apply)

a) Difficulty coordinating schedules
b) Conflicting priorities or goals
c) Lack of clear communication
d) Other (please specify)

9. How do you handle conflicting priorities or competing demands on your time?

a) I prioritize based on urgency and importance
b) I negotiate with stakeholders to adjust expectations
c) I seek guidance from my manager or team
d) I try to do everything and hope for the best

**Section 4: Support and Resources**

10. What resources or support systems do you rely on to manage your workload effectively? (Select all that apply)

a) Training or professional development
b) Mentorship or coaching
c) Time management tools or software
d) Team or departmental support
e) Other (please specify)

11. How satisfied are you with the support and resources provided by our organization to manage workload?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand the challenges and opportunities related to workload management within our organization.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Workload Management:

**Workload Management Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand your experiences and perceptions about workload management within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to enhance workload management.

**Section 1: Current Workload**

1. On average, how many tasks or projects do you typically handle at any given time?

a) 1-3
b) 4-6
c) 7-10
d) More than 10

2. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

a) Rarely
b) Occasionally
c) Frequently
d) Almost always

3. What is the most common type of task or project you handle? (Select all that apply)

a) Routine administrative tasks
b) Special projects or initiatives
c) Customer-facing tasks
d) Team or departmental responsibilities
e) Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Time Management**

4. How do you prioritize your tasks and projects?

a) Based on urgency and importance
b) Based on deadlines and timelines
c) Based on personal preference and interest
d) Based on input from others (e.g., manager, team members)

5. What tools or methods do you use to manage your time effectively? (Select all that apply)

a) To-do lists
b) Calendars
c) Task management software
d) Pomodoro timers
e) Other (please specify)

6. How often do you take breaks or practice self-care to manage stress and workload?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

7. How often do you communicate with your team or manager about your workload and priorities?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Rarely

8. What challenges do you face when collaborating with others on projects or tasks? (Select all that apply)

a) Difficulty coordinating schedules
b) Conflicting priorities or goals
c) Lack of clear communication
d) Other (please specify)

9. How do you handle conflicting priorities or competing demands on your time?

a) I prioritize based on urgency and importance
b) I negotiate with stakeholders to adjust expectations
c) I seek guidance from my manager or team
d) I try to do everything and hope for the best

**Section 4: Support and Resources**

10. What resources or support systems do you rely on to manage your workload effectively? (Select all that apply)

a) Training or professional development
b) Mentorship or coaching
c) Time management tools or software
d) Team or departmental support
e) Other (please specify)

11. How satisfied are you with the support and resources provided by our organization to manage workload?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand the challenges and opportunities related to workload management within our organization.

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral

b) Yes, most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely
e) Never

b) Somewhat high
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat low
e) Very low

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide suggestions)

2. Are there any specific initiatives or programs you'd like to see implemented to enhance our workplace culture?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide suggestions)

**Conclusion:**

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide any additional feedback)

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your opinion and want to understand your experiences and perceptions about our workplace environment. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more comfortable and productive work environment for everyone.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the overall workplace environment?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What do you like most about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What do you like least about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Physical Workspace**

4. How would you rate the cleanliness and organization of your workspace?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Fair, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

5. Are there any physical aspects of your workspace that cause discomfort or distraction? (e.g., lighting, temperature, noise)

(Open-ended text field)

6. Do you have a dedicated workspace or shared workspace? If shared, how do you feel about it?

(1 = Very Positive, 2 = Somewhat Positive, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Negative, 5 = Very Negative)

**Section 3: Social Environment**

7. How would you rate the level of collaboration and teamwork among colleagues?

(1 = Very Low, 2 = Low, 3 = Medium, 4 = High, 5 = Very High)

8. Are there any social or cultural aspects of the workplace that you find uncomfortable or distracting? (e.g., noise levels, office politics)

(Open-ended text field)

9. Do you feel like you have a sense of community or belonging in the workplace?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 4: Technology and Tools**

10. How would you rate the effectiveness of our technology and tools in supporting your work?

(1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Fair, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

11. Are there any technology or tool-related issues that cause frustration or inefficiency?

(Open-ended text field)

12. Do you have the necessary resources and support to perform your job effectively?

(1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

13. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a better workplace environment for everyone.
